## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t, which is the fundamental problem in population dynamics. Classical models range from exponential and logistic growth to more complex density-dependent and time-varying models.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, Malthusian model)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Strong Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population)
- Weak Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P) (depensation without extinction threshold)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (density-dependent with hyperbolic saturation)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (growth with constant removal rate)
- Time-varying logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (seasonal carrying capacity)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (generalized growth curve)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (cubic density effects)
- Exponential with time decay: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (time-varying growth rate)
- Ratio-dependent growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P / (1 + c3 * P) (logistic with predation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear dependence on P (dP_dt ∝ P) → exponential/Malthusian dynamics indicating per-capita rate is constant
- Quadratic P term (P² appears) → density-dependent feedback, typically logistic-type regulation
- Cubic P term or P*(P-a)*(K-P) structure → Allee effect with critical population threshold
- Logarithmic coupling log(P) multiplied by P → Gompertz-type growth with asymmetric approach to carrying capacity
- Rational form P/(1+cP) → saturating density dependence (contest competition vs. scramble competition)
- Additive constant term independent of P → constant immigration/harvesting/stocking effects
- Trigonometric time dependence sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) → seasonal or periodic environmental forcing
- Product of multiple (linear in P) factors → multiple ecological thresholds (Allee, carrying capacity)
- Negative P² coefficient with positive P coefficient → self-limiting growth approaching equilibrium from below
- Explicit time dependence through exponential exp(c*t) → environmental degradation or improvement trends

## GT Analysis

Let me simplify the GT numerical expression:
```
0.17*(−1 + P/1.047)*(1 − P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 − P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 − exp(−0.097*P))*P
```

Let me expand each term:

**Term 1:** `0.17*(−1 + P/1.047)*(1 − P/10.21)*P`
= 0.17*(P/1.047 − 1)*(1 − P/10.21)*P

Let me expand (P/1.047 − 1)(1 − P/10.21):
= P/1.047 − P²/(1.047×10.21) − 1 + P/10.21
= −1 + P(1/1.047 + 1/10.21) − P²/10.69

So Term 1 = 0.17*P*(−1 + P×1.053 − P²×0.0935)
= 0.17*(−P + 1.053P² − 0.0935P³)

**Term 2:** `0.17*(1 − P/10.21)*P`
= 0.17*(P − P²/10.21)
= 0.17P − 0.01665P²

**Term 3:** `0.17*(1 − exp(−0.097P))*P`
= 0.17P − 0.17P*exp(−0.097P)

Combining all terms:
- P³ term: −0.17×0.0935 P³ = −0.0159 P³
- P² term: 0.17×1.053 P² − 0.01665 P² ≈ 0.1790P² − 0.01665P² = 0.1624 P²
- P term: −0.17P + 0.17P + 0.17P = 0.17P
- Exponential term: −0.17P*exp(−0.097P)

So GT ≈ **c₀P³ + c₁P² + c₂P + c₃P·exp(c₄P)**

where c₃P·exp(c₄P) with c₄ < 0.

Now I search for candidates with the structure: P³ + P² + P + P·exp(P).

**Candidates 22, 23:** `P³c₀ + P²c₁ + P²c₂ + Pc₃ + Pc₄exp(Pc₅)` — This is P³c₀ + P²(c₁+c₂) + P(c₃+c₄exp(Pc₅)). This matches the form P³ + P² + P + P·exp(P). ✓

**Candidate 22:** `P³c₀ + P²c₁ + P²c₂ + Pc₃ + Pc₄exp(Pc₅)`
= c₀P³ + (c₁+c₂)P² + c₃P + c₄P·exp(c₅P)

Setting:
- c₀ = −0.0159
- c₁+c₂ = 0.1624
- c₃ = 0.17
- c₄ = −0.17
- c₅ = −0.097

This exactly matches the GT! ✓

**Candidate 21:** `P³c₀ + P²c₁ + Pc₂ + Pc₃exp(Pc₄)` — same structure with fewer redundant parameters. Also matches. ✓

**Candidate 30:** `P³c₀ + P²c₁ + Pc₂ + Pc₃exp(Pc₄) + c₅` — has a constant offset c₅. GT has no constant offset (at P=0, GT=0). Set c₅=0, then same as candidate 21. ✓

**Candidate 27:** `P³c₀ + P²c₁ + Pc₂ + Pc₃exp(Pc₄) + P + c₅` — set c₅=0, absorb P into c₂. ✓

Many candidates match, but let me confirm candidate 22 clearly works since it's clean.

Candidate 22: `P³c₀ + P²c₁ + P²c₂ + Pc₃ + Pc₄exp(Pc₅)` matches perfectly.

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare it with each candidate.

## GT Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
```
0.17*(−1 + P/1.047)*(1 − P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 − P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 − exp(−0.097*P))*P
```

Let me expand this:

**Term 1:** `0.17*(−1 + P/1.047)*(1 − P/10.21)*P`
= 0.17*(P/1.047 − 1)*(1 − P/10.21)*P

Let me denote a = 1/1.047 ≈ 0.955, b = 1/10.21 ≈ 0.098

= 0.17*(aP − 1)*(1 − bP)*P
= 0.17*(aP − abP² − 1 + bP)*P
= 0.17*(aP² − abP³ − P + bP²)
= 0.17*(−abP³ + (a+b)P² − P)

**Term 2:** `0.17*(1 − P/10.21)*P`
= 0.17*(P − bP²)
= 0.17*P − 0.17*b*P²

**Term 3:** `0.17*(1 − exp(−0.097*P))*P`
= 0.17*P − 0.17*P*exp(−0.097*P)

Combining all terms:
- P³ coefficient: −0.17*ab = −0.17/(1.047*10.21) ≈ −0.17*0.0935 ≈ −0.0159
- P² coefficient: 0.17*(a+b) − 0.17*b = 0.17*a = 0.17/1.047 ≈ 0.1623
- P coefficient: −0.17 + 0.17 + 0.17 = 0.17
- Exponential term: −0.17*P*exp(−0.097*P)

So GT = **α*P³ + β*P² + γ*P + δ*P*exp(−λ*P)**

where α, β, γ, δ, λ are specific constants. The key structural elements are:
1. A cubic polynomial in P: `c*P³ + c*P² + c*P`
2. A term: `c*P*exp(c*P)` (with negative exponent coefficient)

No dependence on `t`, no logarithmic terms, no sin terms, no sqrt terms.

Now I need to find candidates that have exactly the structure: **polynomial in P (up to degree 3) + c*P*exp(c*P)**.

Let me scan candidates for this structure:

- **Candidate 32:** P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + Pc3 + Pc4*exp(Pc5) + c6 — has constant c6

The GT has no constant term (at P=0, GT=0). So candidates with a free constant can set it to 0.
